I accidentally spilled water as I was pouring it into my water bottle. I bent over to clean it up off the floor with a napkin and dropped my macaroon. Oops. He asked me,  "What would happen if you pour your coffee on the ground?"
I replied, "You would clean it up."
"Of course I would clean it up, but if you pour out your coffee, you don't get another cup."
After a bit longer discussion, and feeling like pouring my coffee on the ground so he could clean it up, I asked if there is a way to speak to the manager or owner that he made reference to.
My parking meter is run out by now, but no ticket today, thank God!

"Well ma'am, if you dropped it, you dropped it-"
"Okay, thanks. I gotta go. My meter ran out. I don't want a parking ticket."

I like to help out local businesses,  but it is small shops like these that encourage me to continue going to local Starbucks and Coffee Beans. Why? Because great customer service constantly given, without compromise to the product.

<user_name>Thomas Gilles</user_name><time>1597691043835<//time><Rating>1</Rating>< Review>
NEEDS ZERO STARS.
They TOTALLED out my very rare truck!
More concerned about upselling then repairing!

LONG STORY BUT WORTH THE READ.
Took my 2008 King Ranch Expedition EL 4x4 for A/C recharge the summer before this incident to this shop and was told had a slow leak in the condenser but would probably make it through the summer with a freon recharge. At the end of the following summer I had enough with the A/C taking 30-45 minutes of highway driving for the air to get cold. The wife took the truck in and asked them to complete the repairs THEY had diagnosed from before. After also recommending a new radiator, that was very slowly leaking water from the seam, I agreed to the radiator as I was told the A/C condenser was indeed leaking freon and needed to be changed to fix the A/C. The tech and the desk lady both ensured the A/C would be fixed and a future water leak would also be averted; fine. After a week in the shop, I picked up the truck at 10am on a Friday (~80¬∞ outside) and the A/C temp felt exactly the same as it did the week before. Went right back to the shop and they confirmed the A/C system was full of freon BEFORE they started the work!... NOT leaking freon! Why then was $1,300+ of work and parts changed out and no proper diagnosis was made?! The leak they visually identified in the condenser was actually the Power Steering fluid collecting dirt through a very slow leak. Power steering lines run through the A/C condenser in many Fords and notoriously leak. The very rude tech, with metal @#&t hanging from his face, left a hose clamp for the transmission line off the new radiator. This cooked my transmission as I was driving later that day on the freeway when the hose blew off the fitting. The entire paint, underbody and engine bay was drenched in Transmission oil. Hydraulic oil is usually corrosive to paint. So AAA found that the Transmission got damaged when the oil drained out and the truck may possibly have electrical issues and need a new paint job in a few months if the clearcoat starts to peel. So they totalled it out. Left my family of 6 without a vehicle for six months until we could find an equivalent replacement that was CA smog legal. Thanks Auto DIAGNOSTICS for not actually diagnosing my A/C, it cost my family a truck that they all loved. Ended up with a totalled vehicle and A/C was never repaired properly by admission of the shop owner. Thankfully AAA and BofA are great and covered our loses. But nothing repairs this horrible experience as the used replacement vehicle was 2x the cost of the '08 King Ranch.<//Review>

<rate>5</rate><Resp>None</Resp><text>First of all, people looking at the overall rating of this business should read the 1 star reviews.  Most can be discounted because they have nothing to do with the ability or integrity of the company.  If a senior citizen was denied the use of the bathroom while waiting for service to be complete, that was wrong.  Maybe there was a reason for it, like out of order, that they didn't want to give.  I used the restroom there so I know that is not the usual policy.  Those who felt ripped off because they didn't pass, we just had that happen and had to pay on the $10 on the second test, which I think is the cost of the report. No rip off.  The car had not completed the drive cycle after a repair to an emissions system component and thus failed.  After three weeks of trying the drive cycle, numerous unsatisfactory contacts with the dealer, and an offer by the dealer to check it out for $150 and further charges to do a drive cycle, which they said could take four days, and to evaluate the O2 sensor, and  $70 to run the smog test, we went back to Sunny Sky because they would test the not ready, run the drive cycle and evaluate the sensor for $90. As it happened my daughter did the drive cycle for the 15th time on the way there and the sensor was finally ready.  So, she passed smog and paid the $10. And we learned they check fluid levels now too.

I have taken many cars and trucks there over the years when they were on Sierra. We have had older high mileage vehicles that have had recent check engine lights and repairs to the emissions system.  We have never had a problem passing and they always asked if the check engine light was on or anything going on with the vehicle. They informed me that they couldn't test if the light was on and that if the vehicle hadn't been through the drive cycle that it would fail. And I know enough to know that some modifications or lack of repair can be a problem.  They only bad bit of information we got from everyone initially is that just driving the car 50-100 miles will reset the monitors, which is not true for all cars.

I highly and with full confidence recommend Sunny Skys Smog. I have not yet had oil service because they didn't do it on Sierra but will give that a try now, too.<//text>< user>

< text>
I paid 5 - 10 less than what other smog places wanted, and received quality service. Although everyone's expmooerience is different, that day I had dealt with several other shops that were either overcharging, contradicting with visual inspections, and/or just having that "F U pay me" type of attitude.

When I got to Sunnysky smog I was dealt with quickly and wait time was good. In fact the only reason I waited longer then 20 minutes was that the crew working there went above and beyond what was necessary to ensure my car was smogged. For example, they adjusted my throttle instead of sending me home, marked my timing belt for future use, helped me locate an air leak, and  check my catalytic converter serial number against a database to make sure it was legal, at no other cost than 25 minutes. The converter was crucial, as a DIFFERENT smog shop had demanded paperwork to prove it was bought before a law change instead of putting in the extra work to find out. In the end, for less than the competitors, I got superior service compared to previous experiences. I even had a good chat and a laugh at checkout. Highly, highly recommended.< /text>

< review>
Came in on a Saturday in April to get my GF's car smogged - nobody in front of us, and the service was excellent and super friendly, if perhaps a bit slow. It took 45 minutes to smog her 2016 Ford. The building is older, and the waiting room is warm, even when the temps are in the low 80s. They could really stand to put some shades or awnings over the 2 windows on the south side of the waiting room. At checkout, George showed us exactly on our paperwork where the electronic transmission receipt to the DMV was located.

All things considered, five star experience, but one star off for not being (nearly) as efficient as the service we're used to in Phoenix and Denver, where it's a multi-lane drive-through affair with computerized testing and automated rollers - there, we'd be in and out in 20 minutes, even on a busy day.  On the bright side, George asked us if we had their coupon, and joked with us about needing to print it out - he was kidding. Just knowing about the coupon (or saying yes, when he asks if you have it) gets you $15 off the regular price. =)</review>

<rating>2< /rating><user>102405320006617588972</user><Date>1441816861655<//Date><GmapID>0x809467ff55f610b7:0x32e1cb72e1e2fcc3< /GmapID><pictures>None< /pictures><response>None</response>< text>
This has been my goto smog shop the last few times I've needed to have a vehicle smogged.  I dont have any complaints with the smog service but the last time I was in I needed to use the  restroom.

[I'm diabetic and the 3 most common symptoms of diabetes are frequent hunger, frequent thirst, and frequent urination]

I asked the gal if it would be OK if I used the restroom (they have one right inside the office where you pay) and she said "NO, its for employees only".  I told her I am diabetic and explained that I would really appreciate it she would let me use it.

She again said "NO" and told me that the Valero Gas Station on the corner has a restroom and I could go down there and use their's.

To each his own - but for that I PERSONALLY NEVER INTEND TO RETURN

FWIW - I have six children and 9 grandchildren.  So, its not like the gal was saying NO to a kid or someone in their prime.  She was telling a repeat customer  -who's a grandfather - to walk down to the corner Valero to use the restroom.

What business -- where you have to wait to have service to be done  -- treats their customers that way?

If they're smart they will (or perhaps have already changed) their policy.  I am cleaning my desk and I happen to be going through business cards lying around and theirs is one of them.  Even though this happened a few months ago... I told myself at the time I would be sure to write a review and document my experience.  Well, it just so happens seeing their magnetic card - which I tossed in the trash - reminded me to do so.

So - in conclusion I am rating it 2 stars which is DISLIKE.   Although I really HATED the way the gal treated me I want to be fair in saying their performance on the smogging of my vehicles was not an issue.  I just personally don't intend to give them any further business and would not recommend them to my family or friends.< /text>

I came into this shop today for some garbanzo bean flour. I dropped by here as I was in the area. Living west of the 99, I don't patronize this store often due to the drive. < review>
This is a great place with a surprising number of specialty items that you can't find at other places like Sprouts and Trader Joe's.  However, despite the locality and good selection, I have to leave a poor review because the business insists on responding to each review (poor or otherwise) as you will notice when examining this page.  Responding to reviews is exceptionally bad form, and really does more harm than good for the store's reputation, (not to mention it makes potential reviewers a bit apprehensive).  The selection and service should speak for itself, and of course you cannot please every customer.  Without the rather unseemly online aspect, the store is five stars, no question.</review>

<Review>I try to do my part to keep local mom & pop businesses going, so when I moved to this area of town, I recalled that Kristina's was close by and I'd planned on patronizing this store more often even though their items tend to cost a bit more than other places offer them. I remember going to Kristina's with my mom when I was a kid and I used to shop there after taking my son to therapy at Fresno State since it's just down the street. Kristina's has definitely gone downhill. Way downhill.

I've been in Kristina's a hand full of times since moving back and there was almost always an elderly woman there who never looked happy to see me. This time around, she just stared at my visually impaired child's white cane instead of greeting us as we walked in. I asked to use the restroom and she pointed us to another employee who walked us to the back and pointed us to the restroom without a word. A sign said "no public restrooms", which I assumed meant that it was for employees and customers only. I was there to buy something, not use the restroom, but my little girls had to go. When we came out the elderly woman was standing outside the bathroom door waiting for us. Creep much? She told me that from now on when we shop there, we're to use the restrooms at the laundromat across the parking lot. I told her we don't shop there often anyway.

Thanks to her, from now on, we'll be shopping online or at Sprouts or Vitamin Shoppe. We get treated a thousand times better at these other stores and nobody follows us to the restroom and waits outside the door like a freaking creeper. You don't get to talk to me like the help and keep my business.

I'm sure it can't be easy for Kristina's to stay afloat with places like Sprouts, Whole Foods, Trader Joe's and Vitamin Shoppe to compete with, not to mention online health food stores and the fact that even big box stores like Walmart and Target now carry gluten-free and other specialty food items.

I'd suggest you guys ask rude elderly woman to retire if you want to keep your remaining customers. She's driving people away from the look of some of the other reviews here. You've already lost this customer.</Review><pictures>None< /pictures><response>{'time': 1552060098352, 'text': "Grace,\nAs we replied to you in your duplicate review on Yelp, We at Kristina's are saddened to hear that you experienced unsatisfactory service with us.
